<p style="text-align: left">“After attending MindChamps Reading, my son is more confident of himself speaking in groups and in front of his peers. Be it reading, speaking or writing, MindChamps Reading definitely helps him in a way which I can’t do by myself at home.”&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="#" data-featherlight="#readmore1" title="Read More"><u>Read More</u></a></p>
<div style="display: none">
<div id="readmore1" style="max-width: 500px;">
<p>
“After attending MindChamps Reading, my son is more confident of himself speaking in groups and in front of his peers – his shyness is gone. We have also been reading together every night before his bedtime. This has become our bonding time, especially since I’m working during the day. Be it reading, speaking or writing, MindChamps Reading definitely helps him in a way which I can’t do by myself at home.”</p>
<p>– Serene Seah, parent of Xavier Chua</p></div>
</div>
<p style="text-align: left">– <strong>Serene Seah, parent of Xavier Chua</strong></p>
</blockquote>

<p style="text-align: left">“After I enrolled my daughter in the programme, my daughter’s interest to learn has greatly improved, especially in subjects that she did not perform well before Primary 6. Not only did she enhance her own understanding of various subject topics, she was also motivated to do better.”&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<a href="#" data-featherlight="#readmore2" title="Read More"><u>Read More</u></a></p>
<div style="display: none">
<div id="readmore2" style="max-width: 500px;">
<p>
“The MindChamps PSLE Success programme is well-structured and focused in developing a child’s interest, confidence and motivation to prepare effectively for PSLE. Dedicated and experienced subject trainers and a suitable class size were also my considerations when enrolling my daughter, Charmaine.”</p>
<p>“After I enrolled my daughter in the programme, my daughter’s interest to learn has greatly improved, especially in subjects that she did not perform well before Primary 6. Not only did she enhance her own understanding of various subject topics, she was also motivated to do better.”</p>
<p>“Most importantly, my daughter had benefitted from the MindChamps team of exceptional trainers who had put in a tremendous amount of effort to cover the programme’s syllabus as well as to identify and develop the unique strengths of each individual student.”</p>
<p>– Evelyn Seah, parent of Charmaine Neo</p></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
	 jQuery(".InterestedProgramme").click(function(){
	let first_cus = ""
	
var cboxes = document.getElementsByName('InterestedProgramme[]');
    var len = cboxes.length;
    for (var i=0; i<len; i++) {
if(cboxes[i].checked){
	if(first_cus == ""){
		first_cus = cboxes[i].value
	}else{
		first_cus = first_cus.concat(" " +cboxes[i].value)
	}
	
}
    }

jQuery("#ip_hidden").val(first_cus);
  });
</script>
